<div class="content">
<div class="page_title_no_sub"><h1 class="page_title">CPS Pinto-Fialon Graduate Fellowships - multi year</h1></div>
</div>
</div>  </div>
<!-- END .region-page-title-->
<!-- .region-breadcrumb-->
  <div class="region region-breadcrumb col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-5 col-lg-5">

<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><a href="/">Home</a></div>
</div>

<!--#section-main-content-->
<section  class="dexp-section" id="section-main-content">
	<div class="container">
		<div class="row">
			<!-- .region-content-->
<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">
<div id="node-149" class="node node-webform clearfix" about="/cps-pinto-fialon-graduate-fellowships-multi-year" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="CPS Pinto-Fialon Graduate Fellowships - multi year" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p><strong>Eligibility:</strong> Students entering full-time in regular <strong>graduate degree programs</strong> at UC Berkeley who are Portuguese (defined as Portuguese citizens) or of Portuguese descent (defined as being at least 1/4 Portuguese) are eligible. Students must be accepted into a regular PhD or Masters degree program through the regular competitive application process to be eligible for a Pinto-Fialon fellowship.</p>
<p><strong>Deadline:</strong> <strong>March 31st</strong><br />
Departments with student admission dates after the deadline should advise PSP and Graduate Division.</p>
<p>Students must be<strong> nominated by the departments </strong>recommending them for admission to the graduate program. </p>
</div></div></div><form class="webform-client-form webform-client-form-149" enctype="multipart/form-data" action="/cps-pinto-fialon-graduate-fellowships-multi-year" method="post" id="webform-client-form-149" accept-charset="UTF-8"><div><div  class="webform-layout-box horiz webform-component--student-layout-1"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-textfield webform-component--student-layout-1--student-first-name">
  <label for="edit-submitted-student-layout-1-student-first-name">Student First Name <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" type="text" id="edit-submitted-student-layout-1-student-first-name" name="submitted[student_layout_1][student_first_name]" value="" size="60" maxlength="128" class="form-text required" />
</div>
<div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-textfield webform-component--student-layout-1--student-last-name">
  <label for="edit-submitted-student-layout-1-student-last-name">Student Last Name <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" type="text" id="edit-submitted-student-layout-1-student-last-name" name="submitted[student_layout_1][student_last_name]" value="" size="60" maxlength="128" class="form-text required" />
</div>
</div><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-email webform-component--student-email">
  <label for="edit-submitted-student-email">Student Email <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" class="email form-text form-email required" type="email" id="edit-submitted-student-email" name="submitted[student_email]" size="60" />
</div>
<div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-textfield webform-component--nominating-department">
  <label for="edit-submitted-nominating-department">Nominating Department <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" type="text" id="edit-submitted-nominating-department" name="submitted[nominating_department]" value="" size="60" maxlength="128" class="form-text required" />
</div>
<div  class="webform-layout-box horiz webform-component--department-layout"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-textfield webform-component--department-layout--department-contact-name">
  <label for="edit-submitted-department-layout-department-contact-name">Department Contact Name <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" type="text" id="edit-submitted-department-layout-department-contact-name" name="submitted[department_layout][department_contact_name]" value="" size="60" maxlength="128" class="form-text required" />
</div>
<div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-email webform-component--department-layout--department-contact-email">
  <label for="edit-submitted-department-layout-department-contact-email">Department Contact Email <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" class="email form-text form-email required" type="email" id="edit-submitted-department-layout-department-contact-email" name="submitted[department_layout][department_contact_email]" size="60" />
</div>
</div><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-markup webform-component--cover-letter">
 <h3><strong>Cover Letter</strong></h3>
<p>A cover letter from the departmental admissions committee chair or other designated faculty member stating the following:</p>
<ol><li>that the applicant qualifies as a Portuguese citizen or is a US citizen of Portuguese descent (defined as being at least 1/4 Portuguese),</li>
<li>that the department has recommended the student for admission to a graduate degree program,</li>
<li>what other sources of financial support have been secured or are anticipated for the student,</li>
<li>and evaluating the applicant’s academic potential. </li>
</ol>
</div>
<div id="edit-submitted-upload-cover-letter-ajax-wrapper"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-file webform-component--upload-cover-letter">
  <label for="edit-submitted-upload-cover-letter-upload">Upload Cover Letter <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <div class="form-managed-file"><input type="file" id="edit-submitted-upload-cover-letter-upload" name="files[submitted_upload_cover_letter]" size="22" class="form-file" /><input class="btn form-submit" type="submit" id="edit-submitted-upload-cover-letter-upload-button" name="submitted_upload_cover_letter_upload_button" value="Upload" /><input type="hidden" name="submitted[upload_cover_letter][fid]" value="0" />
</div>
 <div class="description">Files must be less than <strong>2 MB</strong>.<br />Allowed file types: <strong>pdf doc docx odt</strong>.</div>
</div>
</div><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-markup webform-component--additional-elements">
 <h3><strong>Additional Elements of Application</strong></h3>
<p>Copies of the following elements of the admissions application form:</p>
<ol><li>statement of purpose,</li>
<li>statement of research interest (if required by the department),</li>
<li>reference letters,</li>
<li>GRE scores (if GREs are required by the nominating department),</li>
<li>transcripts from previous university studies (scanned photocopies acceptable). </li>
</ol>
</div>
<div id="edit-submitted-statement-of-purpose-ajax-wrapper"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-file webform-component--statement-of-purpose">
  <label for="edit-submitted-statement-of-purpose-upload">Statement of Purpose <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <div class="form-managed-file"><input type="file" id="edit-submitted-statement-of-purpose-upload" name="files[submitted_statement_of_purpose]" size="22" class="form-file" /><input class="btn form-submit" type="submit" id="edit-submitted-statement-of-purpose-upload-button" name="submitted_statement_of_purpose_upload_button" value="Upload" /><input type="hidden" name="submitted[statement_of_purpose][fid]" value="0" />
</div>
 <div class="description">Files must be less than <strong>2 MB</strong>.<br />Allowed file types: <strong>pdf doc docx odt</strong>.</div>
</div>
</div><div id="edit-submitted-statement-of-research-interest-ajax-wrapper"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-file webform-component--statement-of-research-interest">
  <label for="edit-submitted-statement-of-research-interest-upload">Statement of Research Interest </label>
 <div class="form-managed-file"><input type="file" id="edit-submitted-statement-of-research-interest-upload" name="files[submitted_statement_of_research_interest]" size="22" class="form-file" /><input class="btn form-submit" type="submit" id="edit-submitted-statement-of-research-interest-upload-button" name="submitted_statement_of_research_interest_upload_button" value="Upload" /><input type="hidden" name="submitted[statement_of_research_interest][fid]" value="0" />
</div>
 <div class="description">Files must be less than <strong>2 MB</strong>.<br />Allowed file types: <strong>pdf doc docx odt</strong>.</div>
</div>
</div><div id="edit-submitted-reference-letters-ajax-wrapper"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-file webform-component--reference-letters">
  <label for="edit-submitted-reference-letters-upload">Reference Letters <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>

</div><div id="block-menu-block-1" class="block block-menu-block">
  <h3 class='headline'>
    BENELUX Program  </h3>
  <span class="brd-headling"></span>

<div class='clearfix'>&nbsp;</div>
<div class="content" class="content">
  <div class="menu-block-wrapper menu-block-1 menu-name-main-menu parent-mlid-0 menu-level-3">

<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-9 col-lg-9">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">
<div id="node-86" class="node node-page clearfix" about="/benelux/courses" typeof="foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="Courses" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>UC-Berkeley is a vibrant scholarly center where several Departments and Programs routinely offer courses related to political, cultural, economic, historical or social aspects of Belgium, the Netherlands and Luxembourg.</p>
<p>Visit their websites for current listings:</p>
<p><a href="http://dutch.berkeley.edu/">Dutch</a><br /><a href="http://french.berkeley.edu/">French</a><br /><a href="http://german.berkeley.edu/">German</a><br /><a href="http://sseas.berkeley.edu/">South and Southeast Asian Studies</a><br /><a href="http://arthistory.berkeley.edu/">History of Art</a><br /><a href="http://complit.berkeley.edu/">Comparative Literature</a><br /><a href="http://africam.berkeley.edu/">African American Studies &amp; African Diaspora Studies</a><br /><a href="http://jewishstudies.berkeley.edu/">Jewish Studies</a><br /><a href="http://filmmedia.berkeley.edu/">Film &amp; Media Studies</a><br /><a href="http://history.berkeley.edu/">History</a><br /><a href="http://polisci.berkeley.edu/">Political Science</a><br /><a href="http://rhetoric.berkeley.edu/">Rhetoric</a><br /><a href="http://ced.berkeley.edu/">City &amp; Regional Planning</a><br /><a href="http://ced.berkeley.edu/academics/architecture/">Architecture</a><br /><a href="http://sociology.berkeley.edu/">Sociology</a><br /><a href="http://www.law.berkeley.edu/">Law</a></p>
</div></div></div>  </div>

  <ul class="links inline"><li class="print_html first last"><a href="/print/86" title="Display a printer-friendly version of this page." class="print-page" rel="nofollow">Printer-friendly version</a></li>
</ul>
  
</div>

</div>
</div></div>

<!-- === node--blogs.tpl.php -->

<div id="node-209" style="margin-top:30px;" class="node node-blogs clearfix post large"  about="/blog/graduate-student-workshop-modern-german-histories" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">
    <div class="post-img media">

<!-- For field of image (set img-style for full-content display mode) -->
    <div class="post-img media blog-image">
      <div class='mediaholder'>
        <div class="field field-name-field-blog-image field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><img typeof="foaf:Image" alt="group photo of IES-Der Kreis graduate student workshop" src="https://ies.berkeley.edu/sites/default/files/grad_german_workshop.jpg" width="1200" height="795" /><blockquote class="image-field-caption">
  <p>Participants at the IES-Der Kreis graduate student workshop</p>
</blockquote>
</div></div></div>      </div>
    </div>



    <div class="post-format">
 
         <h4>Dec</h4>
        <h2>6</h2>

    </div>
    
	<section class="post-content">
    <header class="meta">

 

		   <h2><a href="/blog/graduate-student-workshop-modern-german-histories">
		   Graduate Student Workshop on Modern German Histories</a></h2>
    </header>
	  <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>On December 6, <em>Der Kreis</em>, a graduate student working group sponsored by IES, organized a workshop on “Modern German Histories” held in the conference room of the UC Berkeley Social Science Matrix. Consisting in three panels, the workshop allowed six graduate students from Stanford and UC Berkeley to discuss their work on a wide range of topics. These panels were moderated by Professors Tara Zahra (University of Chicago), Edith Sheffer (Stanford University), and Stefan-Ludwig Hoffmann (UC Berkeley).</p>
<p>Ian Beacock (Stanford University) began with his paper entitled “On Emotions &amp; Political Violence: The Killing of Walther Rathenau.” Through an engagement with parliamentary transcripts, cabinet documents, newspapers, and magazines, Beacock sought to highlight a commonly overlooked debate surrounding political emotions that emerged following the 1922 murder of Walther Rathenau, Germany’s Jewish foreign minister during the time.</p>
<p>Then, Maria DuBois (UC Berkeley) presented her paper “The Man Builds the House, and the Woman Keeps It!: Feminine Probity, Practicality, and Patriotism in the Diaries of Women Travelers and Settlers in East Africa, 1860s-1920s,” in which she illuminated the role of motherhood during Germany’s imperial period.</p>
<p>Sheer Ganor (UC Berkeley) also presented a paper entitled “Forbidden Words, Banished Voices. Jewish Refugees at the Service of BBC Propaganda to Wartime Germany,” which explored the paradoxical importance of Jewish refugees’ positions within the BBC’s German Service in England.</p>
<p>Later, Benjamin Hein (Stanford University) spoke on “Migration Backed Securities. Emigrants Underwrite the New Transatlantic Economy, 1860-1873,” throughout which Hein examined the emigrant-cotton exchange between the American South and Europe and how such transatlantic trade stimulated the growth of Imperial Germany’s economy.</p>
<p>Next, Elena Kempf (UC Berkeley) engaged with the legal imaginations of Henry Dunant and Johann-Caspar Bluntschli in her paper, “War, Law, and Time: Codifying International Humanitarian Law in Late Nineteenth Century France and Germany.”</p>
<p>Finally, Julia Wambach (UC Berkeley) highlighted the influence of the German occupation of France on the French attitudes towards their own occupation of Germany following the Second World War in her paper, “In search of the German resistance: experiences, expectations, and the French occupation of Germany 1945-1955.” In all, the fifteen participants in the day’s proceedings benefited greatly from the opportunity receive constructive feedback on their work as well as to engage in the lively discussions that ensued following these presentations of forthcoming scholarship.</p>
</div></div></div>	</section>
  
</div> 


</div>
</div></div>
<!-- END .region-content-->
		</div>
	</div>

<!-- === node--blogs.tpl.php -->

<div id="node-334" style="margin-top:30px;" class="node node-blogs clearfix post large"  about="/blog/new-program-study-austria" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">
    <div class="post-img media">

              </div>
    </div>

<!-- For field of image (set img-style for full-content display mode) -->
    <div class="post-img media blog-image">
      <div class='mediaholder'>
        <div class="field field-name-field-blog-image field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><img typeof="foaf:Image" alt="Image for Study of Austria Program" src="https://ies.berkeley.edu/sites/default/files/Image%288%29.png" width="4032" height="3024" /><blockquote class="image-field-caption">
  <p>Dr. Markus Schweiger, Executive Director of the Austrian Marshall Plan Foundation, IES Director Jeroen Dewulf, Dr. Wolfgang Petritsch, Director of the Austrian Marshall Plan Foundation, and Dr. Roland Hermann, LL.M.</p>
<div> </div>
</blockquote>
</div></div></div>      </div>
    </div>



    <div class="post-format">
 
         <h4>Feb</h4>
        <h2>21</h2>

    </div>
    
	<section class="post-content">
    <header class="meta">

 

		   <h2><a href="/blog/new-program-study-austria">
		   New Program for the Study of Austria</a></h2>
    </header>
	  <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>The Institute of European Studies at the University of California, Berkeley and the Austrian Marshall Foundation are proud to announce the extension of their cooperation agreement. This will allow us to provide fellowships to a select group of graduate students from the United States and Austria in order to stimulate research in and about the other nation. The agreement also allows for a fruitful cooperation between Austrian universities, research institutes and the University of California.</p>
<p>We are also pleased to inform that with the support of the Marshall Foundation and in cooperation with the Federal Ministry of Science, Research and Economy Education, a new Program initiative for the Study of Austria has been established in the context of the agreement. The goal of the Program is to study Austria-related topics in a European context.</p>
<p>The IES Program for the Study of Austria will integrate the network of Austria Centers around the world, where it will collaborate with the universities of New Orleans, Minneapolis, Edmonton, Leiden, Olmütz, Budapest, Jerusalem, and Vienna. We will participate at the annual convention, which will give two Berkeley graduate students the opportunity to present their work at a local graduate student conference and to have an article on their work published in a publication organized by the University of Vienna. Participating graduate students at the convention will also be invited to the annual German Studies Association.</p>
</div></div></div>	</section>
  
</div> 


</div>
</div></div>

The conference, whose primary goal is to enhance undergraduate knowledge of the European Union and transatlantic relations, allows students from all US institutions with expertise in different fields to interact with each other while networking with international faculty, fostering intercampus cooperation, and recognizing the excellent worked achieved by students at the undergraduate level." />

	<div class="container">

<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">

<!-- === node--blogs.tpl.php -->

<div id="node-424" style="margin-top:30px;" class="node node-blogs clearfix post large"  about="/blog/uc-berkeley-undergraduate-awarded-top-conference-paper-claremont-uc-conference-european-union" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">

<!-- For field of image (set img-style for full-content display mode) -->
    <div class="post-img media blog-image">
      <div class='mediaholder'>
        <div class="field field-name-field-blog-image field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><img typeof="foaf:Image" alt="" src="https://ies.berkeley.edu/sites/default/files/Kim_Gabbitas_and_John_Gleb.JPG" width="4032" height="3024" title="John Gleb (UC Berkeley) and Kim Gabbitas (Univ. of Utah)" /><blockquote class="image-field-caption">
  <div>The winners of the Brussels trip, awarded at the Claremont-UC Undergraduate Research Conference on the European Union: John Gleb (UC Berkeley) and Kim Gabbitas (Univ. of Utah).</div>
</blockquote>
</div></div></div>      </div>
    </div>



    <div class="post-format">
 
         <h4>Apr</h4>
        <h2>6</h2>

    </div>
    
	<section class="post-content">
    <header class="meta">

 

		   <h2><a href="/blog/uc-berkeley-undergraduate-awarded-top-conference-paper-claremont-uc-conference-european-union">
		   UC Berkeley Undergraduate Awarded Top Conference Paper at the Claremont-UC Conference on the European Union</a></h2>
    </header>
	  <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>Each year, IES supports the Claremont-UC Undergraduate Research Conference on the European Union, held at Scripps College. The conference, whose primary goal is to enhance undergraduate knowledge of the European Union and transatlantic relations, allows students from all US institutions with expertise in different fields to interact with each other while networking with international faculty, fostering intercampus cooperation, and recognizing the excellent worked achieved by students at the undergraduate level. Envisioned as an intercampus undergraduate seminar, participating universities simultaneously offer courses on current issues relevant in Europe today, designing curricula so as to encourage student-initiated research and presentations. UC Berkeley was well represented at the 2017 conference, which was held from April 6-8. IES is pleased to announce that one of Berkeley’s talented undergraduates, John Gleb, was distinguished as one of the top two papers of the conference. In addition to having his paper <em>Dividing Germany, Accepting an Invitation to Empire: The Life, Death, and Historical Significance of George Kennan’s ‘Program A’</em> published in the official conference journal, Gleb, along with the recipient of the second top-paper distinction, will have the opportunity to present his research in Brussels during the upcoming summer trip, supported by IES. Congratulations, John!</p>
</div></div></div>	</section>
  
</div> 


</div>
</div></div>

<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">

<!-- === node--blogs.tpl.php -->

<div id="node-210" style="margin-top:30px;" class="node node-blogs clearfix post large"  about="/blog/undergraduate-student-conference-european-studies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">
    <div class="post-img media">
      <div class='mediaholder'>
              </div>
    </div>

<!-- For field of image (set img-style for full-content display mode) -->
    <div class="post-img media blog-image">
      <div class='mediaholder'>
        <div class="field field-name-field-blog-image field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><img typeof="foaf:Image" alt="Group photo of undergraduate conference in European Studies" src="https://ies.berkeley.edu/sites/default/files/2nd_undergrad_conf.jpg" width="1200" height="900" /><blockquote class="image-field-caption">
  <p>Undergraduate conference in European Studies, with the members of the jury and presenters <strong>Nitisha Baronia</strong>, <strong>Kevin Mahoney</strong>, <strong>Ziang Zhou</strong>, and <strong>Yinan Zhang</strong></p>
</blockquote>
</div></div></div>      </div>
    </div>



    <div class="post-format">
 
         <h4>Nov</h4>
        <h2>30</h2>

    </div>
    
	<section class="post-content">
    <header class="meta">

 

		   <h2><a href="/blog/undergraduate-student-conference-european-studies">
		   Undergraduate Student Conference in European Studies</a></h2>
    </header>
	  <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>The European Union Student Ambassador (EUSA) group, an official UC Berkeley student organization supported by IES and the European Commission, hosted its second Undergraduate Conference in European Studies on November 30. During the conference, participants presented research proposals answering the question of whether or not a collective European cultural or political identity exists. These proposals were then judged by a panel of faculty and diplomats. This semester, the team of judges was composed of Maria Ripoll, Higher Education Officer at the French Consulate; Helena Malikova, IES’ current EU fellow who works in the EU Directorate General for Competition; IES Director Jeroen Dewulf, Spanish Studies Program Chair Emilie Bergmann, and IES visiting scholar Max Baumgart (Univ. of Cologne). Four UC Berkeley undergraduate students, Nitisha Baronia, Kevin Mahoney, Ziang Zhou, and Yinan Zhang, along with one Berkeley City College student, Diego Parada, were finalists and presented different perspectives on and interpretations of the question. Ultimately, Baronia, who focused in her paper on the growth of rightwing populism in Europe, was declared the winner. Overall, the event offered a stimulating opportunity for the approximately fifty undergraduates, faculty, and community members in attendance to consider the ever-so-prevalent issues surrounding the formation of a European identity.</p>
</div></div></div>	</section>
  
</div> 


</div>
</div></div>
<!-- END .region-content-->
		</div>
	</div>

<section  class="dexp-section" id="section-bottom" style="background-color:#232D37">

  <div class="region region-left-sidebar col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-3 col-lg-3">

<div class='clearfix'>&nbsp;</div>
<div class="content" class="content">
  <p><a href="/cbs"><img alt="Center for British Studies logo" src="/sites/default/files/shared/images/CBSbridgelogo.jpg" style="margin-top:-10px" /></a></p>

</div><div id="block-menu-block-1" class="block block-menu-block">
  <h3 class='headline'>
    Center for British Studies  </h3>
  <span class="brd-headling"></span>

<div class='clearfix'>&nbsp;</div>
<div class="content" class="content">
  <div class="menu-block-wrapper menu-block-1 menu-name-main-menu parent-mlid-0 menu-level-3">
  <ul class="menu"><li class="first leaf menu-mlid-557"><a href="/cbs/events">Events</a></li>

<!-- .region-content-->
<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-9 col-lg-9">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">
<div id="node-35" class="node node-page clearfix" about="/cbs/courses" typeof="foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="British-Themed Courses" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>UC-Berkeley is a vibrant scholary center whose course offerings regarding Britain, English literature, British visual culture, the British Empire, and modern politics are constantly being revised. Course topics range from the cinema of Alfred Hitchcock to British integration into the EU.</p>
<p>The following departments routinely offer British-themed courses. Visit their websites for current listings:</p>
<p><a href="http://ced.berkeley.edu/academics/architecture/">Architecture</a></p>
<p><a href="http://celtic.berkeley.edu/">Celtic Studies</a></p>
<p><a href="http://complit.berkeley.edu/">Comparative Literature</a></p>
<p><a href="http://english.berkeley.edu/">English</a></p>
<p><a href="http://fm.berkeley.edu/">Film &amp; Media Studies </a></p>
<p><a href="http://history.berkeley.edu/">History</a></p>
<p><a href="http://arthistory.berkeley.edu/">History of Art</a></p>
<p><a href="http://music.berkeley.edu/">Music</a></p>
<p><a href="https://philosophy.berkeley.edu/">Philosophy</a></p>
<p><a href="http://guide.berkeley.edu/undergraduate/degree-programs/political-economy/">Political Economy</a></p>
<p><a href="http://www.polisci.berkeley.edu/">Political Science</a></p>
<p><a href="http://rhetoric.berkeley.edu/">Rhetoric</a></p>
<p><a href="http://sociology.berkeley.edu/">Sociology</a></p>
<p><a href="http://sseas.berkeley.edu/">South and Southeast Asian Studies</a></p>
<p><a href="http://dcrp.ced.berkeley.edu/">City &amp; Regional Planning</a></p>
</div></div></div>  </div>

  <ul class="links inline"><li class="print_html first last"><a href="/print/35" title="Display a printer-friendly version of this page." class="print-page" rel="nofollow">Printer-friendly version</a></li>
</ul>
  
</div>

</div>
</div></div>
<!-- END .region-content-->
		</div>
	</div>
</section>
<!--END #section-main-content-->

      <span property="dc:title" content="CBS Graduate Groups" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><h3><strong>Graduate Groups</strong></h3>
<p> </p>
<h4><strong>ANGLOPHONIA! LITERATURES IN ENGLISH</strong><br />
Contact: Jessica Crewe (jcrewe [at] berkeley.edu)<br /><a href="http://townsendcenter.berkeley.edu/programs/working-group/anglophonia-literatures-english">Website</a></h4>
<p>The group discusses theoretical and methodological questions specific to studies of the legacy of British colonialism in Anglophone literature, politics, and the arts. The biweekly discussions are held at UC Berkeley.<br />
 </p>
<h4><strong>BERKELEY-STANFORD BRITISH STUDIES READING GROUP</strong><br />
Contact: Sam Wetherell (wetherellsam [at] gmail.com)<br /><a href="http://townsendlab.berkeley.edu/berkeley-stanford-british-studies-reading-group">Website</a>
</h4><p>The group discusses recent work in British history in light of developments in cultural studies, imperial and post-colonial history, gender studies, and comparative history. The monthly discussions are held alternately in Berkeley and Stanford. <br />
 
</p><h4><strong>BRITISH SCHOLARS WORKSHOP</strong><br />
Contact:  Julia Shatz (julia.shatz [at] berkeley.edu)<br /><a href="http://townsendlab.berkeley.edu/berkeleys-british-scholars-workshop">Website</a>
</h4><p>The group discusses work-in-progress on topics in British studies and has the aim of introducing younger scholars into the craft of a historian. Discussions take place at UC Berkeley three times a semester.
</p><h4>
<strong>NINETEENTH CENTURY AND BEYOND BRITISH CULTURAL STUDIES</strong><br />
Contact: Marisa Palacios Knox (mknox [at] berkeley.edu)<br /><a href="http://townsendlab.berkeley.edu/nineteenth-century-and-beyond-british-cultural-studies-working-group">Website</a></h4>
<p>Founded in 1995, the Nineteenth-Century and Beyond British Cultural Studies Working Group provides a forum for faculty and graduate students to discuss new research on the literature and culture of the long nineteenth century. Pre-circulated papers investigate issues of aesthetics, politics, history, theory, and other current sites of academic focus.</p>
<p> </p>
<h4><strong>BRITISH POLITICAL ECONOMY</strong><br />
Contact: Alex Dumont (alex_dumont [at] berkeley.edu) and Jesse Cordes Selbin (j.c.s. [at] berkeley.edu]<br /><a href="http://townsendgroups.berkeley.edu/group/british-political-economy">Website</a></h4>
<p>The <em>British Political Economy </em>working group provides a forum in which its members can discuss 18th through early 20th century British political economy in relation to work in the humanities, exploring the interactions of political and economic theories with both works of literature and theories of aesthetics.</p>
</div></div></div>  </div>

  <ul class="links inline"><li class="print_html first last"><a href="/print/36" title="Display a printer-friendly version of this page." class="print-page" rel="nofollow">Printer-friendly version</a></li>
</ul>
  
</div>

</div>
</div></div>

<section  class="dexp-section" id="section-main-content">
	<div class="container">
		<div class="row">
			<!-- .region-left-sidebar-->
  <div class="region region-left-sidebar col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-3 col-lg-3">
    <div id="block-menu-block-2" class="block block-menu-block">
  <h3 class='headline'>
    Graduates  </h3>
  <span class="brd-headling"></span>

<div class='clearfix'>&nbsp;</div>
<div class="content" class="content">
  <div class="menu-block-wrapper menu-block-2 menu-name-main-menu parent-mlid-0 menu-level-2">
  <ul class="menu"><li class="first leaf menu-mlid-520"><a href="/admissions-requirements">Requirements for Admission to the D.E. in European Studies</a></li>
<li class="leaf menu-mlid-521"><a href="/designation-requirements">Requirements for Designation to the D.E. in European Studies</a></li>
<li class="leaf active-trail active menu-mlid-522"><a href="/graduate-education" class="active-trail active">Graduate Education in European Studies</a></li>
<li class="last leaf menu-mlid-525"><a href="/ies-student-working-groups">IES Student Working Groups</a></li>
</ul></div>
</div>
</div>  </div>
<!-- END .region-left-sidebar-->
<!-- .region-content-->
<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-9 col-lg-9">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">
<div id="node-7" class="node node-page clearfix" about="/graduate-education" typeof="foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="Graduate Education in European Studies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>Besides the D.E. in European Studies, IES provides a wide range of other opportunities for graduate students to enhance their coursework, support their research, and create a community of Europeanists. The Disciplinary M.A./Ph.D. in a European Language is available from 7 departments: Classics, French, German, Italian, Scandinavian, Turkish, and  Spanish &amp; Portuguese. The Professional M.A./J.D./Ph.D. with European Studies emphasis is also available to all graduate students in professional programs.  The M.A. in International and Area Studies (MAIAS) is housed in the International and Area Studies Dept. MAIAS is an interdisciplinary degree program for students already matriculating in one of UC Berkeley’s professional schools or academic departments who seek expertise in contemporary international issues and/or detailed knowledge of Europe, its regions or its countries. Matriculating students receive two degrees. Two IES core faculty serve as MAIAS Core Faculty. For more, go to <a href="http://iastp.berkeley.edu/iasgrad">MAIAS</a>.</p>
<p>IES offers a range of fellowships for graduate students. These include: Entering Graduate Student Fellowships, Pre-dissertation and Dissertation Grants for students focusing on Europe, Pre-dissertation grants for students focusing on Lusophone communities and issues, and Pre-Dissertation and Dissertation grants for students focusing on Britain and intending to travel to the UK to either prepare a dissertation proposal or finish their research in the UK, and FLAS awards that support students who will study a modern European language as an integral part of an academic program. For more, go to <a href="http://ies.berkeley.edu/grants/index.html">Grants &amp; Fellowships</a>.</p>
</div></div></div>  </div>

  <ul class="links inline"><li class="print_html first last"><a href="/print/7" title="Display a printer-friendly version of this page." class="print-page" rel="nofollow">Printer-friendly version</a></li>
</ul>
  
</div>

</div>
</div></div>

The D.E. in European Studies starts in the Fall 2016 semester and will be coordinated by the Institute of European Studies in cooperation with the Institute of Slavic, East European, and Eurasian Studies (ISEEES). The D.E. in European Studies provides curricular and research resources for students who want to concentrate on European Studies within their respective disciplines and have their work formally recognized in their degree designation." />

<!-- .region-content-->
<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-9 col-lg-9">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">
<div id="node-4" class="node node-page clearfix" about="/graduate-program" typeof="foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="Graduate Program" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>In Spring 2015, the Graduate Council of University of California, Berkeley established the Designated Emphasis in European Studies. The D.E. in European Studies starts in the Fall 2016 semester and will be coordinated by the Institute of European Studies in cooperation with the Institute of Slavic, East European, and Eurasian Studies (ISEEES). The D.E. in European Studies provides curricular and research resources for students who want to concentrate on European Studies within their respective disciplines and have their work formally recognized in their degree designation. Designed to bring together faculty and students from different departments, the D.E. is administered by the Graduate Group in European Studies and provides a unique context for rigorous cross-disciplinary research. Sponsoring departments include History, Law, Agricultural and Resource Economics, Sociology, Economics, Scandinavian, Anthropology, History of Art, German and Dutch, Political Science, Italian, Architecture, Comparative Literature, Rhetoric, Spanish and Portuguese, Interdisciplinary Studies, Slavic, and French. However, the D.E. is open to interested students regardless of whether their home department is officially affiliated with the D.E. The program helps advance Berkeley’s position as one of the nation’s leading European Studies program and facilitate research in and cooperation with other European universities. Students applying to the D.E. must be prepared to integrate high-level research in European Studies into their coursework, qualifying exam and dissertation.</p>
<p>In order to strengthen the cohesion of the intellectual community within European Studies, the Graduate Group in European Studies is committed to organize extra-curricular activities. Every semester, a “graduate student discussion group in European Studies” and, annually, a “graduate student conference in European Studies” will be organized at the Institute of European Studies in cooperation with its partner institutions, the Institute of Slavic, East European, and Eurasian Studies and the UC Berkeley Social Science Matrix.</p>
<p><strong>Contact us:</strong> </p>
<h3>Executive Committee</h3>
<p><a href="mailto:jdewulf@berkeley.edu">Jeroen Dewulf</a>, Chair<br /><a href="mailto:pog@berkeley.edu">Pierre-Olivier Gourinchas</a><br /><a href="mailto:klinos@berkeley.edu">Katerina Linos</a><br /><a href="mailto:mbevir@berkeley.edu">Mark Bevir</a><br /><a href="mailto:dgokturk@berkeley.edu">Deniz Gokturk</a> <br /><a href="mailto:jfconnel@berkeley.edu">John Connelly</a></p>
<h3>Graduate Advising Committee</h3>
<p><a href="mailto:bux@berkeley.edu">Richard Buxbaum</a>, Head Graduate Advisor<br /><a href="mailto:miafull@berkeley.edu">Mia Fuller</a>, Second Graduate Advisor<br /><a href="mailto:jdewulf@berkeley.edu">Jeroen Dewulf</a> <br />
Graduate student coordinator <a href="mailto:deoadao@berkeley.edu">Deolinda Adao</a></p>
</div></div></div>  </div>

	<div class="container">

<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">
<div id="node-140" class="node node-webform clearfix" about="/ies-center-british-studies-graduate-travel-grant" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="IES Center for British Studies Graduate Travel Grant" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p><strong>Deadline:</strong> The application deadline is <strong>February 1</strong>. </p>
<p>A faculty recommendation is require for this application.  Please direct faculty to send the recommendation to <a href="mailto:ctrbs@berkeley.edu">ctrbs@berkeley.edu</a> </p>
<p>More information on grants and application requirements can be found at the <a href="http://ies.berkeley.edu/cbs/grants.html">Center for British Studies</a> website or by contacting:</p>
<p>Center for British Studies<br />
207 Moses Hall<br />
University of California, Berkeley<br />
Berkeley, CA 94720-2316<br />
510.642.4508 | <em><a href="mailto:ctrbs@berkeley.edu">ctrbs@berkeley.edu</a></em> </p>
</div></div></div><form class="webform-client-form webform-client-form-140" enctype="multipart/form-data" action="/ies-center-british-studies-graduate-travel-grant" method="post" id="webform-client-form-140" accept-charset="UTF-8"><div><div  class="webform-layout-box horiz webform-component--name-layout"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-textfield webform-component--name-layout--first-name">

</div><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-textarea webform-component--description-of-proposed-research-project">

 <div class="form-textarea-wrapper resizable"><textarea required="required" id="edit-submitted-description-of-proposed-research-project" name="submitted[description_of_proposed_research_project]" cols="60" rows="5" class="form-textarea required"></textarea></div>
 <div class="description">500 words max</div>
</div>
<div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-markup webform-component--requirements">
 <p><strong>Application Requirements</strong></p>
<ul><li>Applicants must be registered students at University of California, Berkeley.</li>
<li>Graduate students should be in their second or third years (they should not have advanced to candidacy).</li>
<li>Applicants will be expected to demonstrate how their proposed research is part of the a broader course of study supervised by a member of the faculty.</li>
</ul>
</div>

<section  class="dexp-section" id="section-main-content">
	<div class="container">
		<div class="row">
			<!-- .region-left-sidebar-->
  <div class="region region-left-sidebar col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-3 col-lg-3">
    <div id="block-block-18" class="block block-block">

<div class='clearfix'>&nbsp;</div>
<div class="content" class="content">
  <p><a href="/irish"><img alt="Irish Studies Program logo" src="/sites/default/files/shared/images/irish-studies-logo-260.png" style="height:126px; width:260px" /></a></p>
</div>
</div><div id="block-menu-block-1" class="block block-menu-block">
  <h3 class='headline'>
    Irish Studies Program  </h3>
  <span class="brd-headling"></span>

<div class='clearfix'>&nbsp;</div>
<div class="content" class="content">
  <div class="menu-block-wrapper menu-block-1 menu-name-main-menu parent-mlid-0 menu-level-3">
  <ul class="menu"><li class="first leaf menu-mlid-746"><a href="/irish/news-and-notes">News and Notes</a></li>
<li class="leaf menu-mlid-579"><a href="/irish/affiliated-faculty">Affiliated Faculty</a></li>
<li class="leaf menu-mlid-580"><a href="/irish/events">Events</a></li>
<li class="leaf active-trail active menu-mlid-581"><a href="/irish/courses" class="active-trail active">Courses</a></li>
<li class="leaf menu-mlid-582"><a href="/irish/study-ireland">Study in Ireland</a></li>
<li class="last leaf menu-mlid-583"><a href="/irish/resources-and-links">Resources and Links</a></li>
</ul></div>
</div>
</div>  </div>
<!-- END .region-left-sidebar-->
<!-- .region-content-->
<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-9 col-lg-9">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">
<div id="node-61" class="node node-page clearfix" about="/irish/courses" typeof="foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="Courses" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>The Irish Studies Program at U.C. Berkeley does not offer dedicated courses, but courses on Irish literature, culture, and history are offered regularly in several departments on campus, particularly in the Celtic Studies Program and the English Department.  Here are courses being offered in Fall 2017:</p>
<p>Celtic Studies R1B/2, <a href="http://celtic.berkeley.edu/courses/fall-2017/reading-composition-topic-tba-2/">Reading and Writing about Modern Irish Literature</a>, taught by Zachary Johnson</p>
<p>Celtic Studies 15, <a href="http://celtic.berkeley.edu/courses/fall-2017/elementary-modern-irish/">Elementary Modern Irish</a>, taught by Thomas Walsh</p>
<p>Celtic Studies 70, <a href="http://celtic.berkeley.edu/courses/fall-2017/fall-2017-celtic-studies-70/">The World of the Celts</a>, taught by Dan Melia</p>
<p>Celtic Studies 128, <a href="http://celtic.berkeley.edu/courses/fall-2017/fall-2017-celtic-studies-128/">Medieval Celtic Cultures</a>, taught by Annalee Rejhon</p>
<p>Celtic Studies 168, <a href="http://celtic.berkeley.edu/courses/fall-2017/fall-2017-celtic-studies-168/">Celtic Mythology and Oral Tradition</a>, taught by Annalee Rejhon</p>
<p>English 126, <a href="https://english.berkeley.edu/courses/5442">British Literature, 1900-1945</a>, taught by Catherine Flynn</p>
<p>English 190, <a href="http://Another Day in Purgatory: Irish Literature and the Afterlife">Another Day in Purgatory: Irish Literature and the Afterlife</a>, taught by CFS Creasy</p>
<p>History 103C.001, <a href="http://history.berkeley.edu/courses/undergraduate/2017/fall/103c001">The Making (and Breaking?) of Britain</a>, taught by Jason Rozumalski</p>
<p> </p>
</div></div></div>  </div>

  <ul class="links inline"><li class="print_html first last"><a href="/print/61" title="Display a printer-friendly version of this page." class="print-page" rel="nofollow">Printer-friendly version</a></li>
</ul>
  
</div>

</div>
</div></div>
<!-- END .region-content-->
		</div>
	</div>
</section>
<!--END #section-main-content-->

<div class="content">
<div id="node-148" class="node node-webform clearfix" about="/kirk-underhill-undergraduate-and-graduate-prize" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="Kirk Underhill Undergraduate and Graduate Prize" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p><strong>Nomination deadline: May 31</strong></p>
<p>For any questions for information, please contact:</p>
<p>Center for British Studies<br />
207 Moses Hall<br />
University of California, Berkeley<br />
Berkeley, CA 94720-2316<br />
510.642.4508 | <em><a href="mailto:ctrbs@berkeley.edu">ctrbs@berkeley.edu</a></em> | <a href="http://ies.berkeley.edu/cbs" target="_blank"><strong>ies.berkeley.edu/cbs</strong></a></p>
</div></div></div><form class="webform-client-form webform-client-form-148" enctype="multipart/form-data" action="/kirk-underhill-undergraduate-and-graduate-prize" method="post" id="webform-client-form-148" accept-charset="UTF-8"><div><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-radios webform-component--select-one">
  <label for="edit-submitted-select-one">Select one <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <div id="edit-submitted-select-one" class="form-radios"><div class="form-item form-type-radio form-item-submitted-select-one">

	<div class="container">
		<div class="row">
			<!-- .region-left-sidebar-->
  <div class="region region-left-sidebar col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-3 col-lg-3">
    <div id="block-block-16" class="block block-block">

<div class='clearfix'>&nbsp;</div>
<div class="content" class="content">
  <p><a href="nsp"><img alt="Nordic Studies Program logo" src="/sites/default/files/shared/images/nordic_studies_logo.jpg" style="height:55px; width:200px" /></a></p>
</div>
</div><div id="block-menu-block-1" class="block block-menu-block">
  <h3 class='headline'>
    Nordic Studies Program  </h3>
  <span class="brd-headling"></span>

<div class='clearfix'>&nbsp;</div>
<div class="content" class="content">
  <div class="menu-block-wrapper menu-block-1 menu-name-main-menu parent-mlid-0 menu-level-3">
  <ul class="menu"><li class="first leaf menu-mlid-757"><a href="/nsp/events">Events</a></li>
<li class="leaf menu-mlid-586"><a href="/nsp/grants">Grants and Fellowships</a></li>
<li class="leaf active-trail active menu-mlid-587"><a href="/nsp/courses" class="active-trail active">Courses</a></li>
<li class="last leaf menu-mlid-588"><a href="/nsp/people">People</a></li>
</ul></div>
</div>
</div>  </div>
<!-- END .region-left-sidebar-->
<!-- .region-content-->
<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-9 col-lg-9">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">
<div id="node-69" class="node node-page clearfix" about="/nsp/courses" typeof="foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="Courses" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p><strong>Would you like to study a Nordic language on the UCB campus?</strong></p>
<p>Currently, the Department of Scandinavian offers courses in Danish, Finnish, Icelandic, Norwegian, and Swedish.  A course in the historical Old Norse is also offered.  Danish and Finnish are simultaneously taught as DL (distance learning) courses to other UC campuses whenever the need rises. For information on studying Nordic languages, visit <a href="http://blogs.lscrtest.com/scandinavian/languages/">http://blogs.lscrtest.com/scandinavian/languages/</a>.</p>
<p>You can also visit the Department of Scandinavian Studies <a href="http://scandinavian.berkeley.edu/">website</a>.</p>
</div></div></div>  </div>

  <ul class="links inline"><li class="print_html first last"><a href="/print/69" title="Display a printer-friendly version of this page." class="print-page" rel="nofollow">Printer-friendly version</a></li>
</ul>
  
</div>

</div>
</div></div>
<!-- END .region-content-->
		</div>
	</div>
</section>

<div id="node-279" class="node node-page clearfix" about="/program-directors" typeof="foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="Program Directors" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>

<section  class="dexp-section" id="section-main-content">
	<div class="container">
		<div class="row">
			<!-- .region-content-->
<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">
<div id="node-149" class="node node-webform clearfix" about="/cps-pinto-fialon-graduate-fellowships-multi-year" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="CPS Pinto-Fialon Graduate Fellowships - multi year" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p><strong>Eligibility:</strong> Students entering full-time in regular <strong>graduate degree programs</strong> at UC Berkeley who are Portuguese (defined as Portuguese citizens) or of Portuguese descent (defined as being at least 1/4 Portuguese) are eligible. Students must be accepted into a regular PhD or Masters degree program through the regular competitive application process to be eligible for a Pinto-Fialon fellowship.</p>
<p><strong>Deadline:</strong> <strong>March 31st</strong><br />
Departments with student admission dates after the deadline should advise PSP and Graduate Division.</p>
<p>Students must be<strong> nominated by the departments </strong>recommending them for admission to the graduate program. </p>
</div></div></div><form class="webform-client-form webform-client-form-149" enctype="multipart/form-data" action="/cps-pinto-fialon-graduate-fellowships-multi-year" method="post" id="webform-client-form-149" accept-charset="UTF-8"><div><div  class="webform-layout-box horiz webform-component--student-layout-1"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-textfield webform-component--student-layout-1--student-first-name">
  <label for="edit-submitted-student-layout-1-student-first-name">Student First Name <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" type="text" id="edit-submitted-student-layout-1-student-first-name" name="submitted[student_layout_1][student_first_name]" value="" size="60" maxlength="128" class="form-text required" />
</div>
<div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-textfield webform-component--student-layout-1--student-last-name">
  <label for="edit-submitted-student-layout-1-student-last-name">Student Last Name <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" type="text" id="edit-submitted-student-layout-1-student-last-name" name="submitted[student_layout_1][student_last_name]" value="" size="60" maxlength="128" class="form-text required" />
</div>
</div><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-email webform-component--student-email">
  <label for="edit-submitted-student-email">Student Email <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" class="email form-text form-email required" type="email" id="edit-submitted-student-email" name="submitted[student_email]" size="60" />
</div>
<div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-textfield webform-component--nominating-department">
  <label for="edit-submitted-nominating-department">Nominating Department <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" type="text" id="edit-submitted-nominating-department" name="submitted[nominating_department]" value="" size="60" maxlength="128" class="form-text required" />
</div>
<div  class="webform-layout-box horiz webform-component--department-layout"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-textfield webform-component--department-layout--department-contact-name">
  <label for="edit-submitted-department-layout-department-contact-name">Department Contact Name <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" type="text" id="edit-submitted-department-layout-department-contact-name" name="submitted[department_layout][department_contact_name]" value="" size="60" maxlength="128" class="form-text required" />
</div>
<div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-email webform-component--department-layout--department-contact-email">
  <label for="edit-submitted-department-layout-department-contact-email">Department Contact Email <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <input required="required" class="email form-text form-email required" type="email" id="edit-submitted-department-layout-department-contact-email" name="submitted[department_layout][department_contact_email]" size="60" />
</div>
</div><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-markup webform-component--cover-letter">
 <h3><strong>Cover Letter</strong></h3>
<p>A cover letter from the departmental admissions committee chair or other designated faculty member stating the following:</p>
<ol><li>that the applicant qualifies as a Portuguese citizen or is a US citizen of Portuguese descent (defined as being at least 1/4 Portuguese),</li>
<li>that the department has recommended the student for admission to a graduate degree program,</li>
<li>what other sources of financial support have been secured or are anticipated for the student,</li>
<li>and evaluating the applicant’s academic potential. </li>
</ol>
</div>
<div id="edit-submitted-upload-cover-letter-ajax-wrapper"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-file webform-component--upload-cover-letter">
  <label for="edit-submitted-upload-cover-letter-upload">Upload Cover Letter <span class="form-required" title="This field is required.">*</span></label>
 <div class="form-managed-file"><input type="file" id="edit-submitted-upload-cover-letter-upload" name="files[submitted_upload_cover_letter]" size="22" class="form-file" /><input class="btn form-submit" type="submit" id="edit-submitted-upload-cover-letter-upload-button" name="submitted_upload_cover_letter_upload_button" value="Upload" /><input type="hidden" name="submitted[upload_cover_letter][fid]" value="0" />
</div>
 <div class="description">Files must be less than <strong>2 MB</strong>.<br />Allowed file types: <strong>pdf doc docx odt</strong>.</div>
</div>
</div><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-markup webform-component--additional-elements">
 <h3><strong>Additional Elements of Application</strong></h3>
<p>Copies of the following elements of the admissions application form:</p>
<ol><li>statement of purpose,</li>
<li>statement of research interest (if required by the department),</li>
<li>reference letters,</li>
<li>GRE scores (if GREs are required by the nominating department),</li>
<li>transcripts from previous university studies (scanned photocopies acceptable). </li>
</ol>
</div>
<div id="edit-submitted-statement-of-purpose-ajax-wrapper"><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-file webform-component--statement-of-purpose">

</div><div  class="form-item webform-component webform-component-markup webform-component--information">

207 Moses Hall, MC 2316                       <br />
Berkeley, CA 94720-2316</strong></p>
<p>510.643.0980 (phone message)<br />

<div class="page_title_no_sub"><h1 class="page_title">Undergraduate Education</h1></div>
</div>
</div>  </div>
<!-- END .region-page-title-->

  <div class="region region-breadcrumb col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-5 col-lg-5">

<!--#section-main-content-->
<section  class="dexp-section" id="section-main-content">
	<div class="container">
		<div class="row">
			<!-- .region-content-->
<div class="region region-content col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12">
<div class="tabs"></div><div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">
<div class="content">
<div id="node-2" class="node node-page clearfix" about="/undergraduate-education" typeof="foaf:Document">

  
      <span property="dc:title" content="Undergraduate Education" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><h3>Undergraduate Conference on the European Union</h3>
<p>IES supports the annual Claremont-UC Undergraduate Research Conference on the EU held at Scripps College. The conference is open to all undergraduates in California, and Berkeley always has strong representation. The primary purpose of the conference is to enhance undergraduate training in and knowledge of the European Union and US/European relations and to allow US students with expertise in different areas to interact with each other as well as with international faculty, foster intercampus cooperation, and recognize the excellent work achieved by students. Envisioned as an intercampus undergraduate seminar, the participating campuses simultaneously offer courses on the issues relevant in Europe today and design the curriculum to encourage student initiated research and presentations. Having completed individual projects, students from each participating institution and their faculty mentors gather for an interactive conference focusing on European issues and student research.  Drawing over 50 students annually from institutions across the nation, it is the only known forum for undergraduate students to share their research on the EU.</p>
<h3>Courses</h3>
<p>Political Economy (PE) is one of the six undergraduate majors in the interdisciplinary dept. of International and Area Studies; it offers a Minor in European Studies (ES). PE majors must complete nine upper-division courses including PE 100 and PE 101: both have a primary focus on Europe. A course providing historical context is required—for ES concentrators this might be “Old and New Europe” (History), or “Politics of European Integration” (Poli. Sci.). The remaining four courses comprise the ES concentration and are selected from UC Berkeley’s diverse departments under the guidance of a PE faculty advisor. IES Assoc. Director Crawford serves as its faculty advisor. For more, go to <a href="http://iastp.berkeley.edu/peminor">Minor in European Studies</a>.</p>
<p>A second interdisciplinary undergraduate option for ES concentrators is the Interdisciplinary Studies Field Major (ISF), providing undergraduates the opportunity to develop individual interdisciplinary majors with courses selected from all disciplines under the guidance of an ISF faculty advisor. IES Assoc. Director Crawford is the faculty advisor for ISF students who choose a European focus for their Senior Thesis. For more, go to <a href="http://ls-advise.berkeley.edu/major/isf.html">ISF</a>.</p>
<p>IES coordinates a DeCal course on Europe, taught by students for students. For applications, go the DeCal<a href="http://www.decal.org/courses">website</a>. To learn more about the course, please click <a href="http://ies.berkeley.edu/Why_Europe_Still_Matters_2015_Report.html">here</a>.</p>
<p>IES supports the annual Travel Study course to the Benelux countries in Europe, where students learn about the EU in Brussels and Luxembourg. They also visit the European Investment Bank and the European Parliament. To learn more about this course, please click <a href="http://ies.berkeley.edu/blogs/euro_parliament.html">here</a>.</p>
<h3>Study Abroad</h3>
<p>Study abroad is an unparalleled way of experiencing Europe during your time at UC Berkeley. By engaging firsthand with European people and cultures, you will be able to expand your understanding of European history, language, and contemporary issues, while enriching your studies in new and dynamic ways. UC Berkeley offers study, research, and internship programs in Europe to students from all majors. Summer, semester, and year-long study programs are available, and most programs do not require any language prerequisites.</p>
<ul><li><a href="http://eap.ucop.edu/">UC Education Abroad Program</a></li>
<li><a href="http://summerabroad.berkeley.edu/">UC Berkeley Summer Abroad</a></li>
<li><a href="http://globalinternships.berkeley.edu/">UC Berkeley Global Internships</a></li>
<li><a href="http://gsp.berkeley.edu/">IARU Global Summer Program</a></li>
<li><a href="http://sociology.berkeley.edu/study-abroad-norway">Sociology Norway Study Abroad Program</a></li>
</ul><h3>European Languages</h3>
<p>IES supports the teaching of Less Commonly Taught European Languages (i.e. all European languages with the exception of English, French, German, Italian, Russian and Spanish) on the UC Berkeley campus. It also wants to encourage the use of LCTL library materials for academic research. Currently, undergraduate can learn European languages from seven language departments: Comparative Literature (Greek), French, German (German, Dutch), Italian, Scandinavian Studies (Finnish, Norwegian, Danish, Swedish, Irish/Gaelic, Welsh), Spanish and Portuguese (Spanish, Portuguese, Catalan), and Near Eastern Studies (Turkish). Slavic languages and Eastern European languages are supported by the <a href="http://iseees.berkeley.edu/">Institute of Slavic, East European, and Eurasian Studies</a>. For an overview of all European languages taught on the Berkeley campus, go to our <a href="http://ies.berkeley.edu/europeanlanguages/index.html">European Languages Portal</a>.</p>
<p>IES supports the creation of new European LCTL courses on the Berkeley campus as well as the creation of new courses in existing LCTLs that privilege reading knowledge and new teaching methodologies that facilitate academic research.</p>
<p>IES also wants to encourage students and faculty to use more European LCTLs library materials for academic research. Students, both undergraduate and graduate, and faculty who wish to use Library materials (books, ebooks, graphic novels, dissertations, DVDs, etc.) written in a European LCTL and published in Europe that are currently not available on the Berkeley campus, can fill out the <a href="http://www.lib.berkeley.edu/using-the-libraries/recommend-purchase-form" target="_blank">Library Recommendation Form</a> and mention “IES LCTL Support” in the Comments section. IES provides special funding to the UC Berkeley Library to finance the purchase of these materials. This support only applies to LCTLs that are still spoken in Europe; no support will be given for classical or extinctlanguages nor for Slavic and other Eastern European languages supported by the <a href="http://iseees.berkeley.edu/" target="_blank">Institute of Slavic, East European, and Eurasian Studies</a>.</p>
<p>In cooperation with the <a href="http://iseees.berkeley.edu/">Institute of Slavic, East European, and Eurasian Studies</a>, IES supports the work of the UC Berkeley Library subject specialists to enhance the European collections in general and LCTL collections in particular. For more information on all European collections at the UC Berkeley Library, please contact our subject specialists:</p>
<p><a href="mailto:mburnette@berkeley.edu">Michaelyn Burnette</a> (English and Celtic languages)<br /><a href="http://guides.lib.berkeley.edu/subject-guide/English">English collections</a></p>
<p><a href="mailto:jchurch@library.berkeley.edu">Jim Church </a>(International Documents + EU Depository Library)<br /><a href="http://guides.lib.berkeley.edu/c.php?g=148082">EU Depository Library collections</a></p>
<p><a href="mailto:skhanaka@library.berkeley.edu">Shayee Khanaka</a> (Turkish, Kurdish, and Maltese)</p>
<p><a href="mailto:jott@berkeley.edu">Jeremy Ott</a> (German and European Nordic languages)<br /><a href="http://guides.lib.berkeley.edu/subject-guide/121-German-">German collections</a><br /><a href="http://guides.lib.berkeley.edu/subject-guide/84-Scandinavian-">Scandinavian collections</a></p>
<p><a href="mailto:smendoza@library.berkeley.edu">Steve Mendoza</a> (Dutch)<br /><a href="http://guides.lib.berkeley.edu/subject-guide/83-Dutch">Dutch collections</a></p>
<p><a href="mailto:lpendse@library.berkeley.edu">Liladhar Pendse</a> (Slavic and other Eastern European languages, including Romanian)<br /><a href="http://guides.lib.berkeley.edu/subject-guide/53-Slavic-East-European-Studies">Slavic and Easter European Collections</a></p>
<p><a href="mailto:cpotts@library.berkeley.edu">Claude Potts</a> (Romance languages + Breton and Euskara)<br /><a href="http://guides.lib.berkeley.edu/subject-guide/french-studies">French collections</a><br /><a href="http://guides.lib.berkeley.edu/subject-guide/italian-studies">Italian collections</a><br /><a href="http://guides.lib.berkeley.edu/subject-guide/spanish-portuguese">Spanish and Portuguese collections</a></p>
<h2>URAP</h2>
<p>Through the Undergraduate Research Assistance Program, IES offers undergraduate students an opportunity to do research and to participate at the organization of events about Europe. Students interact with distinguished scholars, journalists and politicians, enrich their resume, and allows them to do a great service to our university and beyond. Every semester, IES looks for motivated students with a strong interest in European Studies to join us. For applications, go to <a href="http://research.berkeley.edu/urap">URAP</a> and look for Institute of European Studies/Professor Jeroen Dewulf.</p>
</div></div></div>  </div>
